				if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
					army_experience = 50
				}
			}					
		}		
		modifier = {

	   	}
		remove_effect = {
			set_technology = { 
				ENG_tech_zygg_sdzz = 1
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_tooltip_zygg_kj_11
		}	
	}

	ENG_mission_London_hhz_zy = {   #左翼回合
		priority = 100
		name = ENG_mission_London_hhz_zy
		icon = eng_trade_unions_support		
		days_mission_timeout = 3
		fire_only_once = no
		visible = {
			tag = ENG			
		}
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		is_good = no
		available = { #完成任务的条件
			has_country_flag = FLAG_ENG_ldwjjs #伦敦危机结束
		}
		activation = { #触发任务的条件（满足这个条件就开始任务）
			always = no
		}
		timeout_effect = {			
			set_country_flag = FLAG_ENG_cywjhh #处于己方回合

			if = { #第一回合ai不行动，其他回合都行动
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						VAR_ENG_London_round_num > 1
					}
					check_variable = { #联盟区由联合阵线控制
						07:gui_display_frame = 1
					}
				}
				ENG_jisuan_London_left_round_end = yes  #联合阵线回合结算
				country_event = ENG_event.393 #左翼回合报告
			}

			if = { #判定政府寄没寄
				limit = {
					not = { #西敏区不由首警司控制
						check_variable = { 
							02:gui_display_frame = 2
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = FLAG_ENG_ldwjjs #伦敦危机结束
				country_event = ENG_event.388 #左翼击败首警司结算事件
			}
			
			activate_mission = ENG_mission_London_hhz_sjs 
			ENG_jisuan_London_blue_round_start = yes  #首警司回合开始

			if = { #第三回合时触发快反政变事件（午夜凶铃）
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						VAR_ENG_London_round_num = 3
					}
				}
				country_event = ENG_event.385
			}
		}
		complete_effect = {                    
			

		}
	}
	ENG_mission_London_hhz_sjs = {   #首警司回合 
		priority = 100
		name = ENG_mission_London_hhz_sjs
		icon = eng_trade_unions_support		
		days_mission_timeout = 5
		fire_only_once = no
		visible = {
			tag = ENG			
		}
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		is_good = no
		available = { #完成任务的条件
			has_country_flag = FLAG_ENG_ldwjjs #伦敦危机结束
		}
		activation = { #触发任务的条件（满足这个条件就开始任务）
			always = no
		}
		timeout_effect = {			
			clr_country_flag = FLAG_ENG_cywjhh #处于己方回合

			
			
			if = { #如果大于第二回合，进入右翼回合，否则进入王党回合
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						VAR_ENG_London_round_num > 2
					}
					check_variable = { #右翼控制格林尼治
						13:gui_display_frame = 4
					}
				}
				ENG_jisuan_London_right_round_start = yes #右翼回合开始
				activate_mission = ENG_mission_London_hhz_yy 
			}
			else = {
				activate_mission = ENG_mission_London_hhz_wd 
			}

			if = { #第一回合时触发黑蔷薇事件
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						VAR_ENG_London_round_num = 1   
					}
				}
				country_event = ENG_event.383
			}
			if = { #第二回合时触发快反入场的两个事件
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						VAR_ENG_London_round_num = 2   
					}
				}
				country_event = ENG_event.384
			}
			#三个攻占地区结算事件
				if = { #判定左翼寄没寄
					limit = {
						not = { #联盟区不由左翼控制
							check_variable = { 
								07:gui_display_frame = 1
							}
						}
					}
					country_event = ENG_event.390 #首警司击败左翼结算事件
				}
				if = { #判定右翼寄没寄
					limit = {
						check_variable = { #回合大于2，不然没刷出来
							VAR_ENG_London_round_num > 2
						}
						not = { #格林尼治不由右翼控制
							check_variable = { 
								13:gui_display_frame = 4 
							}
						}
					}
					country_event = ENG_event.391 #首警司击败右翼结算事件
				}
				if = { #两个都寄了
					limit = {
						not = { #
							check_variable = { 
								07:gui_display_frame = 1
							}
							check_variable = { 
								13:gui_display_frame = 4
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = FLAG_ENG_ldwjjs #伦敦危机结束

					country_event = ENG_event.392 #首警司最终胜利事件
				}
			#	

			
		}
		complete_effect = {                         
		}
	}

					}

					}
				}

			}
